### [163] [GSDrive: Reinforcing Driving Policies by Multi-mode Trajectory Probing with 3D Gaussian Splatting Environment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28111)
*Ziang Guo,Min Chen,Xuefeng Zhang,Yixiao Zhou,Zufeng Zhang,Dzmitry Tsetserukou*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出GSDrive框架，通过3D Gaussian Splatting实现端到端自动驾驶中的物理可微奖励塑造，优化驾驶策略，实验结果优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 端到端自动驾驶面临标注成本高和数据质量随时间降低等问题。现有模仿学习与强化学习结合的方法，由于事件驱动的稀疏延迟奖励，导致学习效果不佳。因此需要新的奖励机制提升策略训练效果。

Method: 本方法构建GSDrive框架，借助3D Gaussian Splatting实现物理可微奖励，通过引入基于flow matching的轨迹预测器，在3DGS模拟器中进行多样化轨迹探查，对候选轨迹即时评估奖励，实现IL与RL的双向知识流。

Result: 在nuScenes重建数据集上的闭环实验中，GSDrive表现优于现有基于仿真的强化学习驾驶方法。

Conclusion: GSDrive有效克服了稀疏延迟奖励带来的策略收敛问题，实现了更优的端到端自动驾驶策略改进，为现实部署提供了更好的解决方案。

Abstract: End-to-end (E2E) autonomous driving presents a promising approach for translating perceptual inputs directly into driving actions. However, prohibitive annotation costs and temporal data quality degradation hinder long-term real-world deployment. While combining imitation learning (IL) and reinforcement learning (RL) is a common strategy for policy improvement, conventional RL training relies on delayed, event-based rewards-policies learn only from catastrophic outcomes such as collisions, leading to premature convergence to suboptimal behaviors. To address these limitations, we introduce GSDrive, a framework that exploits 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) for differentiable, physics-based reward shaping in E2E driving policy improvement. Our method incorporates a flow matching-based trajectory predictor within the 3DGS simulator, enabling multi-mode trajectory probing where candidate trajectories are rolled out to assess prospective rewards. This establishes a bidirectional knowledge exchange between IL and RL by grounding reward functions in physically simulated interaction signals, offering immediate dense feedback instead of sparse catastrophic events. Evaluated on the reconstructed nuScenes dataset, our method surpasses existing simulation-based RL driving approaches in closed-loop experiments. Code is available at https://github.com/ZionGo6/GSDrive.

</details>


### [164] [FreeOcc: Training-Free Embodied Open-Vocabulary Occupancy Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28115)
*Zeyu Jiang,Changqing Zhou,Xingxing Zuo,Changhao Chen*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种全新的、无需训练的开词汇占据预测框架FreeOcc，可在无需3D标注和位姿真值的情况下，基于单目或RGB-D序列，实现对环境的占据预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于学习的占据预测方法需要大量3D标注，且泛化能力较差，难以适应不同环境。作者希望解决对大规模标注的依赖和提升模型无监督泛化能力。

Method: 1. 利用SLAM主干网络估计相机位姿与稀疏几何。
2. 采用几何一致的高斯更新算法，构建稠密3D高斯地图。
3. 利用现成视觉-语言模型，赋予高斯原语开词汇语义。
4. 概率高斯到占据的投影，生成稠密体素占据图。全流程无监督、无需3D标注或位姿真值。

Result: 在EmbodiedOcc-ScanNet数据集上，FreeOcc的IoU与mIoU较现有自监督方法有超过2倍提升。提出并在新基准ReplicaOcc上实验，FreeOcc能直接零样本迁移到新环境，显著优于有监督和自监督基线。

Conclusion: FreeOcc无需训练或标注即可实现跨环境、高精度的开词汇占据预测，极大地降低了数据依赖，提升了方法的通用性和实用性。

Abstract: Existing learning-based occupancy prediction methods rely on large-scale 3D annotations and generalize poorly across environments. We present FreeOcc, a training-free framework for open-vocabulary occupancy prediction from monocular or RGB-D sequences. Unlike prior approaches that require voxel-level supervision and ground-truth camera poses, FreeOcc operates without 3D annotations, pose ground truth, or any learning stage. FreeOcc incrementally builds a globally consistent occupancy map via a four-layer pipeline: a SLAM backbone estimates poses and sparse geometry; a geometrically consistent Gaussian update constructs dense 3D Gaussian maps; open-vocabulary semantics from off-the-shelf vision-language models are associated with Gaussian primitives; and a probabilistic Gaussian-to-occupancy projection produces dense voxel occupancy. Despite being entirely training-free and pose-agnostic, FreeOcc achieves over $2\times$ improvements in IoU and mIoU on EmbodiedOcc-ScanNet compared to prior self-supervised methods. We further introduce ReplicaOcc, a benchmark for indoor open-vocabulary occupancy prediction, and show that FreeOcc transfers zero-shot to novel environments, substantially outperforming both supervised and self-supervised baselines. Project page: https://the-masses.github.io/freeocc-web/.

### [165] [Design and Characteristics of a Thin-Film ThermoMesh for the Efficient Embedded Sensing of a Spatio-Temporally Sparse Heat Source](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28148)
*Sajjad Boorghan Farahan,Ahmed Alajlouni,Jingzhou Zhao*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为ThermoMesh的无源薄膜热电网格传感器，能够通过热传导方式对时空稀疏的热源进行检测和特征分析，具备能效高、灵敏度高等优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高温、恶劣环境下，传统红外成像技术往往受限，而对于如熔滴检测、热点监测等应用场景，亟需一种新型、能效高且能直接嵌入系统的热传感器。现有方案在灵敏度、能耗、集成度等方面仍有不足，因此本文提出新结构以应对上述挑战。

Method: 作者设计了一种带有线性或非线性（如NTC陶瓷、VO2）层间电阻的新型热电网格传感器，并围绕单点（1-稀疏）事件进行了建模与优化。通过对不同结构网格的数值建模，评估其灵敏度分布、最低灵敏度的提升，以及在40dB噪声环境下的定位准确度和温度误差等性能指标。

Result: 仿真结果表明，线性电阻提升16x16网格的最低灵敏度约10倍。使用NTC陶瓷层的200x200网格最低灵敏度提高约14,500倍、VO2层提高约24倍。VO2情况下定位准确率98%，温度误差0.23K，NTC陶瓷情况下无定位误差，温度误差1.83K，噪声等效温度分别为0.07K和1.49K。

Conclusion: ThermoMesh展现出卓越的嵌入式高能效热检测能力，特别适用于传统红外成像受限的严苛场景，如熔滴和热点监测等，有望广泛应用于高温/复杂环境下的实时热管理。

Abstract: This work presents ThermoMesh, a passive thin-film thermoelectric mesh sensor designed to detect and characterize spatio-temporally sparse heat sources through conduction-based thermal imaging. The device integrates thermoelectric junctions with linear or nonlinear interlayer resistive elements to perform simultaneous sensing and in-sensor compression. We focus on the single-event (1-sparse) operation and define four performance metrics: range, efficiency, sensitivity, and accuracy. Numerical modeling shows that a linear resistive interlayer flattens the sensitivity distribution and improves minimum sensitivity by approximately tenfold for a $16\times16$ mesh. Nonlinear temperature-dependent interlayers further enhance minimum sensitivity at scale: a ceramic negative-temperature-coefficient (NTC) layer over 973--1273~K yields a $\sim14{,}500\times$ higher minimum sensitivity than the linear design at a $200\times200$ mesh, while a VO$_2$ interlayer modeled across its metal--insulator transition (MIT) over 298--373~K yields a $\sim24\times$ improvement. Using synthetic 1-sparse datasets with white boundary-channel noise at a signal-to-noise ratio of 40~dB, the VO$_2$ case achieved $98\%$ localization accuracy, a mean absolute temperature error of $0.23$~K, and a noise-equivalent temperature (NET) of $0.07$~K. For the ceramic-NTC case no localization errors were observed under the tested conditions, with a mean absolute temperature error of $1.83$~K and a NET of $1.49$~K. These results indicate that ThermoMesh could enable energy-efficient embedded thermal sensing in scenarios where conventional infrared imaging is limited, such as molten-droplet detection or hot-spot monitoring in harsh environments.

### [166] [FlexiTac: A Low-Cost, Open-Source, Scalable Tactile Sensing Solution for Robotic Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28156)
*Binghao Huang,Yunzhu Li*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: FlexiTac是一种低成本、开源、可扩展的机器人末端执行器用压阻式触觉传感解决方案，具备灵活传感板和多通道读出板，适用于实时控制和大规模数据采集，并支持目前前沿的触觉学习任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器人触觉传感器往往成本高、难以大规模部署或集成度低，且手工制造工艺较复杂，难以保证重复性和量产，难以满足多样化机器人平台的实际需求。

Method: 提出了FlexiTac模块，包括薄型、柔性的三层叠层（FPC-Velostat-FPC）触觉传感板，通过集成柔性电路直接制备电极图案，大幅提升产能与一致性，读出板采用廉价通用组件，支持多通道同步信号采集并通过串口实时传输；可灵活装配于多种末端执行器，无需大量机械改造。

Result: FlexiTac已在多种传感板形式（如指尖贴片与大面积触觉垫）与平台上成功部署，表现出优良的灵活适应性和易用性，且可无缝嵌入现代深度触觉学习任务（如3D视觉-触觉融合、跨机械体技能迁移及仿真微调等）。

Conclusion: FlexiTac为机器人触觉感知提供了低成本、易制造、高适配性的解决方案，有力推动了大规模、可扩展的触觉研究和下游应用的发展。

Abstract: We present FlexiTac, a low-cost, open-source, and scalable piezoresistive tactile sensing solution designed for robotic end-effectors. FlexiTac is a practical "plug-in" module consisting of (i) thin, flexible tactile sensor pads that provide dense tactile signals and (ii) a compact multi-channel readout board that streams synchronized measurements for real-time control and large-scale data collection. FlexiTac pads adopt a sealed three-layer laminate stack (FPC-Velostat-FPC) with electrode patterns directly integrated into flexible printed circuits, substantially improving fabrication throughput and repeatability while maintaining mechanical compliance for deployment on both rigid and soft grippers. The readout electronics use widely available, low-cost components and stream tactile signals to a host computer at 100 Hz via serial communication. Across multiple configurations, including fingertip pads and larger tactile mats, FlexiTac can be mounted on diverse platforms without major mechanical redesign. We further show that FlexiTac supports modern tactile learning pipelines, including 3D visuo-tactile fusion for contact-aware decision making, cross-embodiment skill transfer, and real-to-sim-to-real fine-tuning with GPU-parallel tactile simulation. Our project page is available at https://flexitac.github.io/.

### [167] [RopeDreamer: A Kinematic Recurrent State Space Model for Dynamics of Flexible Deformable Linear Objects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28161)
*Tim Missal,Lucas Domingues,Berk Guler,Simon Manschitz,Jan Peters,Paula Dornhofer Paro Costa*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种新型神经网络框架，用于更准确高效地预测和控制可变形线性物体（DLOs），在仿真任务中显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前DLO操控存在高维、非线性动态和保持拓扑完整性的难题。现有数据驱动方法如RNN和GNN在处理交叉、打结和非物理变形时效果不好，亟需突破。

Method: 提出融合递归状态空间模型（RSSM）和四元数运动链表征的潜在动力学框架，通过将DLO状态编码为相对旋转（四元数）序列，物理上保证链长不变。采用双解码器架构，将状态重建与未来预测任务解耦，强制潜变量学习变形物理规律。

Result: 在大规模含复杂交叉的DLO仿真挑拣轨迹数据集上，模型在50步开环预测误差上较现有方法下降40.52%，推理时间缩短31.17%，并且在多重交叉场景下保持更优的拓扑一致性。

Conclusion: 新方法有效提升了DLO操作的预测精度和效率，可作为复杂长时操控任务的基础模块，展现出扎实的物理合理性和泛化性能。

Abstract: The robotic manipulation of Deformable Linear Objects (DLOs) is a fundamental challenge due to the high-dimensional, non-linear dynamics of flexible structures and the complexity of maintaining topological integrity during contact-rich tasks. While recent data-driven methods have utilized Recurrent and Graph Neural Networks for dynamics modeling, they often struggle with self-intersections and non-physical deformations, such as tangling and link stretching. In this paper, we propose a latent dynamics framework that combines a Recurrent State Space Model with a Quaternionic Kinematic Chain representation to enable robust, long-term forecasting of DLO states. By encoding the DLO as a sequence of relative rotations (quaternions) rather than independent Cartesian positions, we inherently constrain the model to a physically valid manifold that preserves link-length constancy. Furthermore, we introduce a dual-decoder architecture that decouples state reconstruction from future-state prediction, forcing the latent space to capture the underlying physics of deformation. We evaluate our approach on a large-scale simulated dataset of complex pick-and-place trajectories involving self-intersections. Our results demonstrate that the proposed model achieves a 40.52% reduction in open-loop prediction error over 50-step horizons compared to the state-of-the-art baseline, while reducing inference time by 31.17%. Our model further maintains superior topological consistency in scenarios with multiple crossings, proving its efficacy as a compositional primitive for long-horizon manipulation planning.

</details>


### [168] [LaST-R1: Reinforcing Action via Adaptive Physical Latent Reasoning for VLA Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28192)
*Hao Chen,Jiaming Liu,Zhonghao Yan,Nuowei Han,Renrui Zhang,Chenyang Gu,Jialin Gao,Ziyu Guo,Siyuan Qian,Yinxi Wang,Peng Jia,Chi-Wing Fu,Shanghang Zhang,Pheng-Ann Heng*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为LaST-R1的视觉-语言-动作（VLA）统一框架，通过在动作执行前引入物理动态链式推理（CoT）及新型强化学习算法LAPO，实现了物理推理和动作控制的紧密结合。该方法在LIBERO基准上，获得了99.8%的平均成功率，并在现实任务中超过了现有最佳方法，表现出极强的泛化与鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前VLA方法虽然引入了推理机制，但大多局限于静态模仿学习，适应性和泛化能力有限。即使部分引入了强化学习，优化对象仍局限于动作空间，而忽略了底层物理推理过程。因此有必要开发将物理推理动态与动作控制联合优化的新方法。

Method: 作者提出了LaST-R1框架，引入了隐式链式推理（Latent CoT），在动作执行前推理物理动态。提出了Latent-to-Action Policy Optimization（LAPO）算法，该算法联合优化隐式推理过程和动作生成。同时设计了自适应隐式CoT机制，可根据环境复杂度动态调整推理深度。在训练中，先通过一次监督学习预热，然后用LAPO进行强化学习训练。

Result: 在LIBERO基准测试中，LaST-R1仅用一次监督预热，即可达到99.8%的平均成功率，大幅提升了收敛速度和效果。在四个现实机器臂任务（包括单臂和双臂）中，LAPO强化训练后性能相比预热策略可提升44%。还在模拟和现实环境下展现了良好的泛化能力。

Conclusion: LaST-R1通过将物理推理融入决策过程，显著提升了VLA模型在复杂机器人操作任务中的表现。新算法LAPO强化了推理与动作执行间的联系，提升了模型鲁棒性和环境适应能力。这为通用型机器人智能体的研究带来了新的思路。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have increasingly incorporated reasoning mechanisms for complex robotic manipulation. However, existing approaches share a critical limitation: whether employing explicit linguistic reasoning that suffers from latency and discretization, or utilizing more expressive continuous latent reasoning, they are predominantly confined to static imitation learning that limits adaptability and generalization. While online reinforcement learning (RL) has been introduced to VLAs to enable trial-and-error exploration, current methods exclusively optimize the vanilla action space, bypassing the underlying physical reasoning process. In this paper, we present \textbf{LaST-R1}, a unified VLA framework that integrates latent Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning over physical dynamics prior to action execution, along with a tailored RL post-training paradigm. Specifically, we propose \textbf{Latent-to-Action Policy Optimization (LAPO)}, a novel RL algorithm that jointly optimizes the latent reasoning process and the action generation. By bridging reasoning and control, LAPO improves the representation of physical world modeling and enhances robustness in interactive environments. Furthermore, an \textbf{adaptive latent CoT mechanism} is introduced to allow the policy to dynamically adjust its reasoning horizon based on environment complexity. Extensive experiments show that LaST-R1 achieves a near-perfect 99.8\% average success rate on the LIBERO benchmark with only one-shot supervised warm-up, significantly improving convergence speed and performance over prior state-of-the-art methods. In real-world deployments, LAPO post-training yields up to a 44\% improvement over the initial warm-up policy across four complex tasks, including both single-arm and dual-arm settings. Finally, LaST-R1 demonstrates strong generalization across simulated and real-world environments.

### [169] [OmniRobotHome: A Multi-Camera Platform for Real-Time Multiadic Human-Robot Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28197)
*Junyoung Lee,Sookwan Han,Jeonghwan Kim,Inhee Lee,Mingi Choi,Jisoo Kim,Wonjung Woo,Hanbyul Joo*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了OmniRobotHome平台，能够在家庭环境中实现多机器人与多人的实时协作感知和操作，解决了传统方法在实时3D跟踪和遮挡鲁棒性上的瓶颈，推动了多主体协作领域的实验研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 家庭环境中人与多个机器人需要并发协作，且任务往往穿插进行，对空间和时间的依赖极为紧密。但现有系统因遮挡、状态变化快等问题，难以实现鲁棒的、实时的3D感知，从而限制了相关实验的深入。

Method: 作者开发了OmniRobotHome平台：用48台硬件同步的RGB摄像机实现无标记、抗遮挡的多人及多物体3D追踪，并与两台Franka机械臂进行时间同步，实现机器人在真实场景状态下的交互操作，同时持续采集一致世界坐标下的行为轨迹以辅助长期行为建模。

Result: 新平台实现了房间规模下的实时3D跟踪和多机器人协作；实验针对安全共处和人的意图预测两个核心问题，验证了实时感知和历史行为记忆能显著提升协作效率与安全性。

Conclusion: OmniRobotHome首次使得多主体（多机器人多人员）家庭环境下的实验性研究变得可行，有助于推进人-机器人多方协作领域，尤其在安全和前瞻性协作方面展现出提升潜力。

Abstract: Human-robot collaboration has been studied primarily in dyadic or sequential settings. However, real homes require multiadic collaboration, where multiple humans and robots share a workspace, acting concurrently on interleaved subtasks with tight spatial and temporal coupling. This regime remains underexplored because close-proximity interaction between humans, robots, and objects creates persistent occlusion and rapid state changes, making reliable real-time 3D tracking the central bottleneck. No existing platform provides the real-time, occlusion-robust, room-scale perception needed to make this regime experimentally tractable. We present OmniRobotHome, the first room-scale residential platform that unifies wide-area real-time 3D human and object perception with coordinated multi-robot actuation in a shared world frame. The system instruments a natural home environment with 48 hardware-synchronized RGB cameras for markerless, occlusion-robust tracking of multiple humans and objects, temporally aligned with two Franka arms that act on live scene state. Continuous capture within this consistent frame further supports long-horizon human behavior modeling from accumulated trajectories. The platform makes the multiadic collaboration regime experimentally tractable. We focus on two central problems: safety in shared human-robot environments and human-anticipatory robotic assistance, and show that real-time perception and accumulated behavior memory each yield measurable gains in both.

</details>
